\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Receive own Frames in Half-\/\+Duplex mode enabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} MAC MII loopback disabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Full-\/\+Duplex mode selected

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} IPv4 and TCP/\+UDP/\+ICMP frame Checksum Offload disabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Retry Transmission enabled for half-\/duplex mode

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Automatic PAD/\+CRC strip disable

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} half-\/duplex mode retransmission Backoff time\+\_\+limit = 10 slot time

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} half-\/duplex mode Deferral check disabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Receive all frames disabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Source address filtering (on the optional MAC addresses) disabled

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Do not forward control frames that do not pass the address filtering

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Perfect address filtering for unicast addresses

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Drops frames with with TCP/\+IP checksum errors

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Store and forward mode enabled for receive

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Threshold TXFIFO level set to 64 bytes (used when threshold mode is enabled)

\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Disable forwarding frames with errors (short frames, CRC,...)
